[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Stress at work in JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "STRESS_AT_WORK",
        "NAME": "Stress at Work Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "Do you often feel stressed at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, often"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Never"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What are the main causes of stress at work for you?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Heavy workload"},
              {"ANSWER": "Lack of control"},
              {"ANSWER": "Unclear expectations"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your overall stress level at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "1 (Low)"},
              {"ANSWER": "2"},
              {"ANSWER": "3"},
              {"ANSWER": "4"},
              {"ANSWER": "5 (High)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "Have you experienced any physical symptoms of stress at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, often"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Never"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "What strategies do you use to manage stress at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Prioritize tasks"},
              {"ANSWER": "Take regular breaks"},
              {"ANSWER": "Communicate with colleagues"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire aims to assess the level of stress at work, identify the main causes of stress, and gather information on how employees manage stress. The questions are designed to be engaging and easy to understand, with a mix of multiple-choice and rating-scale questions.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"}
            ]
          },
          {

              {"ANSWER": "Uncomfortable"}

            "CODE": "WE_6",
            "NAME": "Do you have access to necessary resources and equipment in your workspace?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, always"},
              {"ANSWER": "Mostly"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "WE_7",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall satisfaction with your workspace?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Dissatisfied"}
            ]
          }

      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire assesses the respondent's perception of their workplace environment, covering aspects such as cleanliness, comfort, noise level, lighting, temperature, and access to resources. The questions are designed to be engaging and easy to understand, with a mix of single-answer and multi-answer options.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Remote working experience

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Remote working experience in the JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "RWE",
        "NAME": "Remote Working Experience",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "RWE1",
            "NAME": "Have you ever worked remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "RWE2",
            "NAME": "What motivated you to start working remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Flexibility and work-life balance"},
              {"ANSWER": "Increased productivity"},
              {"ANSWER": "Reduced commuting time"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "RWE3",
            "NAME": "What are the biggest challenges you face while working remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Staying motivated and focused"},
              {"ANSWER": "Lack of social interaction"},
              {"ANSWER": "Difficulty separating work and personal life"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "RWE4",
            "NAME": "How do you currently manage your work and personal life while working remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Create a dedicated workspace"},
              {"ANSWER": "Establish a routine and schedule"},
              {"ANSWER": "Prioritize self-care and wellness"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "RWE5",
            "NAME": "What tools or software do you use to stay organized and productive while working remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 5,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Project management tools (e.g. Trello, Asana)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Time tracking software (e.g. Harvest, Toggl)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Communication tools (e.g. Slack, Zoom)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "RWE6",
            "NAME": "How do you handle distractions and interruptions while working remotely?",
            "TYPE_ID": 8,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Create a schedule and stick to it"},
              {"ANSWER": "Use noise-cancelling headphones or music"},
              {"ANSWER": "Take regular breaks and practice self-care"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire aims to gather information about the respondent's remote working experience, including their motivation for starting remote work, the challenges they face, and how they manage their work and personal life. It also asks about the tools and software they use to stay organized and productive, and how they handle distractions and interruptions.

Generate me a questionnaire on End of working relationship

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is a sample questionnaire on End of working relationship:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "EWR001",
        "NAME": "End of Working Relationship Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "EWR001Q1",
            "NAME": "What was the reason for the end of your working relationship?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Termination of employment contract"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Resignation"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Downsizing"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "EWR001Q2",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your overall experience with the organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Excellent"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Good"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Fair"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Poor"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "EWR001Q3",
            "NAME": "What do you think was the most significant factor that contributed to the end of your working relationship?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Lack of job satisfaction"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Poor management"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Lack of opportunities for growth and development"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "EWR001Q4",
            "NAME": "Would you recommend the organization to others?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather feedback from employees who have experienced the end of their working relationship with an organization. It asks questions about the reason for the end of the relationship, the employee's overall experience with the organization, the most significant factor that contributed to the end of the relationship, and whether the employee would recommend the organization to others.

              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}

            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.

            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.

            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the instructor's presentation style?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What did you find most engaging or interesting about the course session?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Theoretical concepts"},
              {"ANSWER": "Real-life examples"},
              {"ANSWER": "Interactive activities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "What suggestions do you have for improving the course session?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "More hands-on activities"},
              {"ANSWER": "More time for Q&A"},
              {"ANSWER": "Different presentation style"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire consists of 4 questions, each with a different type:

1. Q1: A multiple-choice question asking learners what they learned from the course session.
2. Q2: A rating question asking learners to rate the instructor's presentation style.
3. Q3: A multiple-choice question asking learners what they found most engaging or interesting about the course session.
4. Q4: An open-ended question asking learners for suggestions on improving the course session.

The questionnaire is designed to gather feedback from learners on their experience with the course session, including what they learned, what they found engaging, and what they would like to see improved.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - Topic: Teambuilding initiatives feedback
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Teambuilding initiatives feedback

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire in JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "TB_FEEDBACK",
        "NAME": "Teambuilding Initiatives Feedback",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "TB_Q1",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall effectiveness of the teambuilding initiative?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not Very Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at All Effective"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TB_Q2",
            "NAME": "What did you enjoy most about the teambuilding initiative?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "The team's camaraderie"},
              {"ANSWER": "The activities and games"},
              {"ANSWER": "The food and refreshments"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TB_Q3",
            "NAME": "What did you find least enjoyable about the teambuilding initiative?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "The team's dynamics"},
              {"ANSWER": "The activities and games"},
              {"ANSWER": "The food and refreshments"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TB_Q4",
            "NAME": "How likely are you to recommend this teambuilding initiative to your colleagues?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Likely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Likely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not Very Likely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at All Likely"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather feedback on teambuilding initiatives. It includes four questions:

1. How would you rate the overall effectiveness of the teambuilding initiative? (Rating scale: Very Effective, Somewhat Effective, Not Very Effective, Not at All Effective)
2. What did you enjoy most about the teambuilding initiative? (Multiple-choice: The team's camaraderie, The activities and games, The food and refreshments, Other (please specify))
3. What did you find least enjoyable about the teambuilding initiative? (Multiple-choice: The team's dynamics, The activities and games, The food and refreshments, Other (please specify))
4. How likely are you to recommend this teambuilding initiative to your colleagues? (Rating scale: Very Likely, Somewhat Likely, Not Very Likely, Not at All Likely)

The questionnaire is designed to be easy to understand and complete, with a mix of rating and multiple-choice questions to gather both quantitative and qualitative feedback.

Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Training and Development Programs:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "TDP_001",
        "NAME": "Training and Development Programs Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "What is your current level of job satisfaction?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Dissatisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very Dissatisfied"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "Have you received any training or development programs in the past 6 months?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, I received training on [insert topic]"},
              {"ANSWER": "No, I did not receive any training"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the effectiveness of the training programs you have attended?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Ineffective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very Ineffective"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "What type of training or development programs would you like to see offered in the future?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Leadership Development"},
              {"ANSWER": "Technical Skills Training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Communication Skills Training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Time Management Training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "How important is it for you to have opportunities for professional growth and development?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not Very Important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at All Important"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather information about employees' experiences with training and development programs, their opinions on the effectiveness of these programs, and their suggestions for future training opportunities. The questionnaire includes a mix of multiple-choice and open-ended questions to gather both quantitative and qualitative data.

Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Training and Development Programs:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "TDP_001",
        "NAME": "Training and Development Programs",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "TDP_001_Q1",
            "NAME": "How often do you participate in training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Daily"},
              {"ANSWER": "Weekly"},
              {"ANSWER": "Monthly"},
              {"ANSWER": "Quarterly"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TDP_001_Q2",
            "NAME": "What motivates you to participate in training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "To improve job performance"},
              {"ANSWER": "To gain new skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "To advance in career"},
              {"ANSWER": "To stay updated with industry trends"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TDP_001_Q3",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the effectiveness of our current training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not very effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all effective"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "TDP_001_Q4",
            "NAME": "What type of training or development programs would you like to see offered in the future?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Technical skills training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Leadership development"},
              {"ANSWER": "Communication skills training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Industry-specific training"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has 4 questions, each with a different type:

1. Q1: Multiple-choice question (TYPE_ID: 1) to gauge the frequency of participation in training and development programs.
2. Q2: Multiple-choice question (TYPE_ID: 2) to understand what motivates employees to participate in training and development programs.
3. Q3: Rating question (TYPE_ID: 3) to assess the effectiveness of current training and development programs.
4. Q4: Open-ended question (TYPE_ID: 4) to gather feedback on what type of training or development programs employees would like to see offered in the future.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
